/*          A 6-byte block header, the value chosen arbitrarily          as 0x314159265359 :-).  A 32 bit value does not really          give a strong enough guarantee that the value will not          appear by chance in the compressed datastream. For a compressed file of size 100Gb -- about 100000 blocks --          only a 48-bit marker will do.
